<section class="homepage__about-happyrail">
<div class="homepage__about-happyrail-inner">
<h1 class="homepage__about-happyrail-title">One Platform, All Trains</h1>
<p>As of now, you can book train tickets to 35,000 destinations in <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a href="en/train-tickets" style="color:#ffffff;text-decoration:underline;">Europe</a></span> and beyond. And this is just the beginning. Our dream is to enable online reservation for train tickets from Lisbon to Ho Chi Minh, the world's longest rail journey at 17.852 km.</p>
<p>At HappyRail we believe the fun should start before you step onto the train. Enjoy booking a ticket right where you are. No need to stand in a queue at the station or piece together a complicated puzzle between different providers.</p>
<p>Our mission is to make cross-border travel as easy as possible. We want to take the stress out of your booking experience. Basically, whenever you book with HappyRail your reservation will be cheap, fast and super easy.</p>
<p>Besides all train tickets, we also offer all <span style="text-decoration:underline;"><a href="en/rail-passes" style="color:#ffffff;text-decoration:underline;">rail passes</a></span>! Booking an InterRail, Eurail or Japan Rail Pass has never been this easy.</p>
<p><strong><span id="result_box" lang="en"><span title="Happyrail.">HappyRail. Book your train just as easy as your flight</span><span title="Treintickets net zo makkelijk boeken als vliegtickets.">. It all begins here.</span></span></strong></p>
</div>
</section>

                                    United Kingdom                                 </h2>
<div class="homepage__country-actions">
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/great-britain-by-train">Tickets</a>
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/britrail">Passes</a>
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/british-trains">Trains</a>
</div>
<div class="homepage__country-description">
<p>Book all cheap train tickets in the UK, from London to Manchester or Cornwall to York; and internationally from London to Paris, Brussels and Amsterdam. You can also book all rail passes in the UK, like Britrail, Eurail and Interrail </p>
</div>
</section>
</li>
<li class="homepage__countries-list-item">
<section class="homepage__country">
<img alt="Russia" class="homepage__country-image" src="https://cdn.happyrail.com/images/resized/150/uploads/landingpage_images/moscow_6.jpg"/>
<h2 class="homepage__country-title">
                                    Russia                                 </h2>
<div class="homepage__country-actions">
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/russia-by-train">Tickets</a>
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/eurail">Passes</a>
<a class="homepage__country-actions-btn" href="en/sapsan">Trains</a>
</div>
<div class="homepage__country-description">
<p>Russia has an extensive rail network. All major destinations are connected by long-distance night trains. Travel from Moscow to Irkutsk in 4 days or to Vladiwostok in 7 or 8 days. Between Moscow and St Petersburg you can take the best night train in Russia ("number 1 and 2"), book 1st class to have a meal included. Also a high speed connection between the two biggest cities, the Sapsan. </p>
</div>
</section>
</li>
</ul>
</section>
